< text>
It's very good when it is made as requested. I've been here a dozen or so times, and have ordered twice on UberEats. Generally it is what is to be expected from a poke bowl restaurant. The biggest issue is inconsistency of how they construct their bowls. Depending on who is making it, at times they don't really listen to what you're asking for even though they are only a few feet away. It leaves you frustrated enough to let them just select whatever they want and be ok with it. Additionally, if using UberEats they don't have customization options set-up at all, so only one topping is available for selection in any category. They also don't read any specific requests utilizing UberEats either. I've tried to call the restaurant itself, but the number listed on Google is a cell phone that isn't answered.

Unfortunately I likely won't continue to eat there with any consistancy because you more often than not don't get what you ask/pay for.<//text>

I was referred to Okuma through a couple of friends. This was our first time using a broker and the overall experience was excellent! The short version: the process could not be easier and I had a better feeling compared to dealing with the dealership directly after the purchase. The detailed version: Went to the company‚Äôs website and filled out an application (previous night). One of the brokers (Ken) called me back the next day asking for a few more details about what features we were looking for on the car. Also asked what dealerships we visited and if we already test drove a car (so he could make it clear to the dealer he wasn‚Äôt stealing us away from them). At the time we had a vehicle to trade in/sell. A form was e-mailed us shortly asking for some information regarding the condition of the car and a few pictures. Within a day or two, Ken called back saying there was a car available and quoted us a price that was about $3K less than sticker price. We needed some time to look into our financial details and complete the form for trading in/selling the car. After we finally analyzed our expenses, we told Ken we were willing to go through with the purchase (ended up not using Okuma to sell our car, not on them at all). update aug 2018
bed bug remedies - diatomaceous earth - trap entrance for bugs, buy your own bed frame and bed, can find cheaper alternatives,

have a bed bug trap deterrant on every bed post leg - (they harbor on beds - also seep in in low lighting from breeders in waves),

there are sticky glue traps to trap bugs (highly effective - hard to reach places - entrances - random places)

< text>
My dog is my whole world. Thus, I did not take the decision of who their vet would be lightly. We have visited a vast number of vets from Nipomo all the way to SLO over the last ten years for all three of our pets. All have been satisfying and often absolutely wonderful. However, Animal Care Clinic is on its own level.

We stumbled upon ACC by chance. My dog was having a crazy case of Pancreatitis. He wouldn't get up to eat/drink/go on a walk, leaving me scared and stressed with how to help him since I had no idea what was going on. I called our primary vet explained the severity and they couldn't get me in that day. I called our backup vet and they had no availability. Finally I just drove to ACC (where I had never been) with my sick dog and they MADE TIME FOR HIM right then knowing that it was imperative he receive treatment as soon as possible.

Not only did my dog get immediate treatment for this emergency, afterwards Dr. Barber called every couple days for over a week to check on him. She sent detailed hand written notes home with us for how to make his recovery the most successful. Since then, we have brought all of our pets to ACC and have made Dr. Barber our primary vet. We feel comfortable with her and trust her.

As amazing as Dr. Barber is, she isn't alone. It is the entire team (S/O to Karla and Kate) that make you feel comfortable and as if you were apart of the family. The team clearly talks you through the cost of everything before proceeding so you aren't stuck with a giant surprise bill at the end of your visit. I appreciate the transparency.

Quick Summary:
In my opinion, after visiting many vets, I can confidently say Animal Care Clinic is the best veterinary team on the Central Coast.</text>

< review>
This place came highly recommended and I had really high expectations. I have a service animal and wanted to make sure they had experience with working dogs. Which they did. When I made our initial appointment, they made a really big deal about my bringing my dog's records ahead of her appointment so that they could review them prior to our appointment. Once we got there, we had to wait about 45 minutes, which wasn't a huge deal because we had the last appointment of the day. What was disappointing was that it quickly became apparent that they had not read my dog's medical records and were asking all these questions that were noted on her paperwork. I had some questions which I was told the vet would be calling me back with some answers, but she never did.
There were treats everywhere for the dogs and coffee and tea for the humans. I am all for treats for dogs, but I didn't appreciate that they were out in the lobby for anyone to grab since my working dog does not get food rewards. She was simply more distracted in an already difficult situation for her... and while the vet was great with my dog, the fact that the customer service side of it wasn't so great, I am not sure we will be going back.</review>

<username>Erika Butterfield< /username><Date>1517032806187</Date><userid>107272401253473466210</userid>< rate>

<Gmap_id>0x80ecf0d49b8c5353:0x8acbab68e178a42c</Gmap_id>< review>
I was on my way to visit a friend, driving through the night, when I noticed a hard spot on my dog. I used the "just answer" website, sending photos and communicating with a veterinarian through email. All the arrows pointed to a tumor, which obviously didn't really sit well with me. The friend I was visiting suggested I tried the clinic her two small dogs go to, and I was not disappointed.
The office was large and mostly quiet. They had a separate area that cat owners to go, to not panic their feline friends with all the excited pups. Kate at the front desk was very nice, well informed, and offered some calming stuff for my dog, when she started to get anxious waiting in the loby. The vet tech came out to inform me that they were running a bit behind, and gave me an estimated time to be seen. I was able to leave the lobby and allow my dog to take in all the smells outside she was excited for. They called my cell phone well under the expected timing, to let me know they were ready. The vet tech was very nice, she listened to all my concerns and when the doctor came in, it's like she hit the play back button on fast forward in a way more professional manner.  I was impressed by her listening skills, memmory, and over all professionalism. The doctor was also very polite. She took care  to try to make my dog feel comfortable. She didn't jump to the immediate conclusion that my dog had a tumor, even though she agreed that it sounded alot like so. She still took the time and energy to dig deeper into the issue, and while the symptoms were odd and and a bit out of place, the actually diagnosis was way less frightening! We were all able to figure it all out there together, which made me feel way better about it too.
This amazing service with these bright smiling faces, was all while knowing I would not be a returning customer. They all gave me great advice, and piece of mind while I take my pooch on the road with me.

**side note- I worked at a very well known animal hospital in the past, and I must say that you don't come across genuine people like this at most hospitals. Even at the smaller locally owned vets, we have been treated like a convayer belt. At this clinic, they made the extra effort to make me feel like they actually cared,  and that goes a long way in this business.

5 stars!<//review>

< Review>
TLDR: Excellent prices, excellent service, professional work. This is the place to go for any tire related anything, and is now my personal go-to for tires that I would recommend to everyone.

Full review:

I have been to several tire places and this one is the best of the lot without question.

I called ahead to make sure they had what I needed, as the vehicle in question has uncommon tires. There was a short wait while stock was confirmed, and was subsequently pleasantly suprised to hear the not only did they have 4 tires of the correct size, but they were able to undercut their competitions price.

There is no reduction of quality of service and work from the lower price, which is a definite win in my book. It did take longer than one might expect, but that was due to my tires being really wide as well as run-flat tires, which adds a significant degree of difficulty (have done tires myself in the past with a manual tire machine, so have a bit of experience in this area). Despite the difficulty,  the work was done with no complaints and the team of two brothers worked together very well to complete the job to perfection. They realised that the work was taking a while without me saying anything, and proceeded to explain exactly what was going on without any prompting at all, which shows their professionalism and knowledge in action.

After all was said and done, I was told to bring my car right back if there were any issues and they would take care of it. These guys rock!

2 Months Later: As happy now as on day 1; my truck needs tires soon and I know exactly who to call!

7 Months Later: Awesomely epic service, 'nuff said</Review>

<UserId.>108453675463629554167<//UserId.>< review>
Pizza is average in taste. Pizza menu covers all the usual pizza favorites, including for vegan and vegetarians. Casual eatery. Can buy either by the slice or a whole pie in person, over the phone, online, and on Door Dash.

Soda is one size, one price with free refills.

One of the few places in Downtown San Jose that is opened late throughout the week.

Street parking only. Walking distance to SJSU.< /review>

< Rating>
4< /Rating>
< Review>
I've been to Pizza My Heart a couple times now. I consider myself a big pizza fan, and I can get pretty excited about certain pizza places. I'm lucky in my hometown to have a large variety of different style pizza joints. There's one kind though that I feel is under represented and that's why I love visiting San Jose. I get excited for Pizza by the Heart because of a couple main things. The first thing I enjoy about this place is the size of the slices. These things are huge, and I think the average person can get a good meal with one slice, but you really need more than just one! The other thing I especially like about Pizza by the Heart is how messy these slices can be. You'll have grease dripping down your fingers, dripping down your chin.. it's a mess. I love it though, a huge greasy slice of pizza. Some might have an issue with the amount of grease or mess you get with these slices, but I love it.. many others do, this place can get pretty busy. I'm a creature of habit and always get the same type of pizza, so I can safely say pepperoni is good. The other flavours you'll have to see for yourself. One star deducted because it's really tough to do a perfect pizza. 4 stars is great though.< /Review>

<review>Pizza My Heart is one the best pizza places in DTSJ. The location is perfect if you're a student, or finishing up a day of shopping. The staff are friendly, competent, and capable. I was there last Friday. My girlfriend and I each ordered a slice. After the cashier discovered he had burned our pizza a bit, he apologized and offered the burned slices along with our new ones. That may not seem like a huge deal, but I was happy that he offered.

Eating in the restaurant is pretty standard. Unless the place is packed with students, the  volume never goes above a dull roar. The pizza is delicious (I reccomend the Big Sur if you've never tried it), and the prices are fairly reasonable. If you're in the area, it's definitely worth a try.</review><userid>113574879543280950076< /userid>< rating>
